\DoxyCodeLine{00114\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Define\ RAPIDXML\_STATIC\_POOL\_SIZE\ before\ including\ rapidxml.hpp\ if\ you\ want\ to\ override\ the\ default\ value.}}
